+    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True, nullable=False)  # Whether this assembly definition is active
+    effective_from = Column(DateTime, nullable=True)  # BOM effective from date
+    effective_to = Column(DateTime, nullable=True)  # BOM effective to date
+    yield_factor = Column(Numeric(6,4), nullable=True, default=1.0)  # Output efficiency (1.0 = 100%)
+    notes = Column(Text, nullable=True)  # Assembly notes
+    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
+    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.datetime.utcnow)
+
+    # Relationships
+    parent_product = relationship("Product", foreign_keys=[parent_product_id], back_populates="assemblies_as_parent")
+    lines = relationship("AssemblyLine", back_populates="assembly", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
+    
+    __table_args__ = (
+        UniqueConstraint("parent_product_id", "assembly_code", "version", name="uq_assembly_version"),
+        Index("ix_assemblies_primary", "parent_product_id", "is_primary", "is_active"),
+    )
+
+class AssemblyLine(Base):
+    """Assembly line items - components of an assembly."""
+    __tablename__ = "assembly_lines"
+    id = uuid_column()
+    assembly_id = Column(String(36), ForeignKey("assemblies.id"), nullable=False, index=True)
+    component_product_id = Column(String(36), ForeignKey("products.id"), nullable=False)
+    quantity = Column(Numeric(12, 3), nullable=False)  # Quantity per parent
+    sequence = Column(Integer, nullable=False)  # Order of operations
+    unit = Column(String(10), nullable=True)  # Display unit (EA, L, kg, etc.)
+    is_energy_or_overhead = Column(Boolean, default=False)  # Non-tracked cost adder
+    notes = Column(Text, nullable=True)  # Line-specific notes
+    
+    # Relationships
+    assembly = relationship("Assembly", back_populates="lines")
+    component_product = relationship("Product")
+    
+    __table_args__ = (
+        UniqueConstraint("assembly_id", "sequence", name="uq_assembly_line_sequence"),
+        Index("ix_assembly_line_assembly", "assembly_id"),
+    )
 
 class ProductChannelLink(Base):
     __tablename__ = "product_channel_links"

+def assembly_to_response(assembly: Assembly, db: Session) -> AssemblyResponse:
+    """Convert Assembly model to response DTO."""
+    stmt = (
+        select(AssemblyLine)
+        .options(joinedload(AssemblyLine.component_product))
+        .where(AssemblyLine.assembly_id == assembly.id)
+        .order_by(AssemblyLine.sequence)
+    )
+    lines = db.execute(stmt).scalars().unique().all()
+    
+    # Calculate total cost from component products
+    total_cost = Decimal("0")
+    for line in lines:
+        if line.component_product:
+            # Get usage cost or purchase cost from component product
+            component = line.component_product
+            unit_cost = component.usage_cost_ex_gst or component.purchase_cost_ex_gst or Decimal("0")
+            total_cost += line.quantity * unit_cost
+    
+    return AssemblyResponse(
+        id=str(assembly.id),
+        parent_product_id=assembly.parent_product_id,
+        assembly_code=assembly.assembly_code,
+        assembly_name=assembly.assembly_name,
+        version=assembly.version,
+        is_primary=assembly.is_primary,
+        is_active=assembly.is_active,
+        effective_from=assembly.effective_from,
+        effective_to=assembly.effective_to,
+        yield_factor=assembly.yield_factor,
+        notes=assembly.notes,
+        created_at=assembly.created_at,
+        updated_at=assembly.updated_at,
+        lines=[
+            AssemblyLineResponse(
+                id=str(line.id),
+                assembly_id=str(line.assembly_id),
+                component_product_id=line.component_product_id,
+                quantity=line.quantity,
+                sequence=line.sequence,
+                unit=line.unit,
+                is_energy_or_overhead=line.is_energy_or_overhead,
+                notes=line.notes
+            )
+            for line in lines
+        ],
+        total_cost=total_cost
+    )
+

+# Assembly Definition CRUD Endpoints

+@router.get("/", response_model=List[AssemblyResponse])
+async def list_assemblies(
+    skip: int = Query(0, ge=0),
+    limit: int = Query(100, ge=1, le=1000),
+    parent_product_id: Optional[str] = Query(None),
+    assembly_code: Optional[str] = Query(None),
+    is_active: Optional[bool] = Query(None),
+    db: Session = Depends(get_db)
+):
+    """List assemblies with optional filtering."""
+    stmt = select(Assembly)
+    
+    if parent_product_id:
+        stmt = stmt.where(Assembly.parent_product_id == parent_product_id)
+    
+    if assembly_code:
+        stmt = stmt.where(Assembly.assembly_code.contains(assembly_code))
+    
+    if is_active is not None:
+        stmt = stmt.where(Assembly.is_active == is_active)
+    
+    stmt = stmt.order_by(Assembly.assembly_code, Assembly.version.desc()).offset(skip).limit(limit)
+    assemblies = db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()
+    
+    return [assembly_to_response(a, db) for a in assemblies]
+
+
+@router.get("/{assembly_id}", response_model=AssemblyResponse)
+async def get_assembly(assembly_id: str, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Get assembly by ID."""
+    assembly = db.get(Assembly, assembly_id)
+    if not assembly:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
+            detail="Assembly not found"
+        )
+    
+    return assembly_to_response(assembly, db)
+
+
+@router.post("/", response_model=AssemblyResponse, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
+async def create_assembly(assembly_data: AssemblyCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Create a new assembly with lines."""
+    # Validate parent product exists
+    product = db.get(Product, assembly_data.parent_product_id)
+    if not product:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
+            detail=f"Product {assembly_data.parent_product_id} not found"
+        )
+    
+    # Check if code/version exists
+    existing = db.execute(
+        select(Assembly).where(
+            Assembly.parent_product_id == assembly_data.parent_product_id,
+            Assembly.assembly_code == assembly_data.assembly_code,
+            Assembly.version == assembly_data.version
+        )
+    ).scalar_one_or_none()
+    
+    if existing:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT,
+            detail=f"Assembly {assembly_data.assembly_code} version {assembly_data.version} already exists"
+        )
+    
+    # If setting as primary, deactivate other primaries for this parent
+    if assembly_data.is_primary:
+        existing_primaries = db.execute(
+            select(Assembly).where(
+                Assembly.parent_product_id == assembly_data.parent_product_id,
+                Assembly.is_primary == True
+            )
+        ).scalars().all()
+        for existing_primary in existing_primaries:
+            existing_primary.is_primary = False
+    
+    # Create assembly
+    assembly = Assembly(
+        id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
+        parent_product_id=assembly_data.parent_product_id,
+        assembly_code=assembly_data.assembly_code,
+        assembly_name=assembly_data.assembly_name,
+        version=assembly_data.version,
+        is_primary=assembly_data.is_primary,
+        is_active=assembly_data.is_active,
+        effective_from=assembly_data.effective_from,
+        effective_to=assembly_data.effective_to,
+        yield_factor=assembly_data.yield_factor,
+        notes=assembly_data.notes
+    )
+    db.add(assembly)
+    db.flush()
+    
+    # Create lines
+    for line_data in assembly_data.lines:
+        # Validate component product exists
+        component = db.get(Product, line_data.component_product_id)
+        if not component:
+            raise HTTPException(
+                status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
+                detail=f"Component product {line_data.component_product_id} not found"
+            )
+        
+        line = AssemblyLine(
+            id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
+            assembly_id=assembly.id,
+            component_product_id=line_data.component_product_id,
+            quantity=line_data.quantity,
+            sequence=line_data.sequence,
+            unit=line_data.unit,
+            is_energy_or_overhead=line_data.is_energy_or_overhead,
+            notes=line_data.notes
+        )
+        db.add(line)
+    
+    db.commit()
+    db.refresh(assembly)
+    
+    return assembly_to_response(assembly, db)
+
+
+@router.put("/{assembly_id}", response_model=AssemblyResponse)
+async def update_assembly(assembly_id: str, assembly_data: AssemblyUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Update assembly header and lines."""
+    assembly = db.get(Assembly, assembly_id)
+    if not assembly:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
+            detail="Assembly not found"
+        )
+    
+    # If setting as primary, deactivate other primaries for this parent
+    if assembly_data.is_primary is not None and assembly_data.is_primary:
+        existing_primaries = db.execute(
+            select(Assembly).where(
+                Assembly.parent_product_id == assembly.parent_product_id,
+                Assembly.is_primary == True,
+                Assembly.id != assembly_id
+            )
+        ).scalars().all()
+        for existing_primary in existing_primaries:
+            existing_primary.is_primary = False
+    
+    # Update header fields
+    if assembly_data.assembly_name is not None:
+        assembly.assembly_name = assembly_data.assembly_name
+    if assembly_data.is_primary is not None:
+        assembly.is_primary = assembly_data.is_primary
+    if assembly_data.is_active is not None:
+        assembly.is_active = assembly_data.is_active
+    if assembly_data.effective_from is not None:
+        assembly.effective_from = assembly_data.effective_from
+    if assembly_data.effective_to is not None:
+        assembly.effective_to = assembly_data.effective_to
+    if assembly_data.yield_factor is not None:
+        assembly.yield_factor = assembly_data.yield_factor
+    if assembly_data.notes is not None:
+        assembly.notes = assembly_data.notes
+    
+    # Update lines if provided
+    if assembly_data.lines is not None:
+        # Delete existing lines
+        stmt = select(AssemblyLine).where(AssemblyLine.assembly_id == assembly.id)
+        existing_lines = db.execute(stmt).scalars().all()
+        for line in existing_lines:
+            db.delete(line)
+        
+        db.flush()
+        
+        # Add new lines
+        for line_data in assembly_data.lines:
+            component = db.get(Product, line_data.component_product_id)
+            if not component:
+                raise HTTPException(
+                    status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
+                    detail=f"Component product {line_data.component_product_id} not found"
+                )
+            
+            line = AssemblyLine(
+                id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
+                assembly_id=assembly.id,
+                component_product_id=line_data.component_product_id,
+                quantity=line_data.quantity,
+                sequence=line_data.sequence,
+                unit=line_data.unit,
+                is_energy_or_overhead=line_data.is_energy_or_overhead,
+                notes=line_data.notes
+            )
+            db.add(line)
+    
+    db.commit()
+    db.refresh(assembly)
+    
+    return assembly_to_response(assembly, db)
+
+
+@router.post("/{assembly_id}/set-primary")
+async def set_primary_assembly(assembly_id: str, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Set assembly as primary, deactivating other primaries for the same parent."""
+    assembly = db.get(Assembly, assembly_id)
+    if not assembly:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
+            detail="Assembly not found"
+        )
+    
+    # Deactivate other primaries for this parent
+    existing_primaries = db.execute(
+        select(Assembly).where(
+            Assembly.parent_product_id == assembly.parent_product_id,
+            Assembly.is_primary == True,
+            Assembly.id != assembly_id
+        )
+    ).scalars().all()
+    for existing_primary in existing_primaries:
+        existing_primary.is_primary = False
+    
+    # Set this one as primary
+    assembly.is_primary = True
+    
+    db.commit()
+    db.refresh(assembly)
+    
+    return assembly_to_response(assembly, db)
+
+
+@router.delete("/{assembly_id}", status_code=status.HTTP_204_NO_CONTENT)
+async def delete_assembly(assembly_id: str, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Delete assembly (soft delete by setting is_active=False)."""
+    assembly = db.get(Assembly, assembly_id)
+    if not assembly:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
+            detail="Assembly not found"
+        )
+    
+    assembly.is_active = False
+    db.commit()
+

+@router.post("/{batch_id}/release", response_model=BatchResponse)
+async def release_batch(batch_id: str, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
+    """Release a batch - explodes formula into components."""
+    batch = db.get(Batch, batch_id)
+    if not batch:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
+            detail="Batch not found"
+        )
+    
+    # Use BatchingService to release the batch
+    try:
+        service = BatchingService(db)
+        released_batch = service.release_batch(batch_id)
+        db.commit()
+        db.refresh(released_batch)
+        return batch_to_response(released_batch)
+    except ValueError as e:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_422_UNPROCESSABLE_ENTITY,
+            detail=str(e)
+        )
+    except Exception as e:
+        db.rollback()
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
+            detail=f"Failed to release batch: {str(e)}"
+        )

+class AssemblyCreate(BaseModel):
+    """Create assembly request."""
+    parent_product_id: str
+    assembly_code: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=50)
+    assembly_name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=200)
+    version: int = Field(1, ge=1)
+    is_primary: bool = False
+    is_active: bool = True
+    effective_from: Optional[datetime] = None
+    effective_to: Optional[datetime] = None
+    yield_factor: Optional[Decimal] = Field(1.0, ge=0, le=2.0)
+    notes: Optional[str] = None
+    lines: List[AssemblyLineCreate] = Field(..., min_length=1)
+
+
+class AssemblyUpdate(BaseModel):
+    """Update assembly request."""

+    effective_to: Optional[datetime] = None

+

+from sqlalchemy import inspect

+def _has_archived_column(db: Session, table_name: str = "formulas") -> bool:
+    """Check if the is_archived column exists in the table."""
+    try:
+        # Use get_bind() for SQLAlchemy 1.4+ compatibility
+        engine = db.get_bind() if hasattr(db, 'get_bind') else db.bind
+        inspector = inspect(engine)
+        columns = [col['name'] for col in inspector.get_columns(table_name)]
+        return 'is_archived' in columns
+    except Exception:
+        # If we can't inspect, assume column doesn't exist yet
+        return False
+

+def _get_inventory_summary(product_id: str, db: Session) -> Optional[InventorySummaryResponse]:
+    """Helper to get inventory summary for a product."""
+    try:
+        inventory_service = InventoryService(db)

+def product_to_response(product: Product, db: Optional[Session] = None, include_inventory: bool = False) -> ProductResponse:

+    supplier_name = None

+            from app.adapters.db.models import Supplier
+            supplier = db.get(Supplier, product.supplier_id)

+                supplier_name = supplier.name

     line_total_inc_tax = round_money(line_total_ex_tax + tax_amount)

+
+
+# Costing Domain Rules
+
+class CostSource(str, Enum):
+    """Source of cost information."""
+    FIFO_ACTUAL = "fifo_actual"
+    SUPPLIER_INVOICE = "supplier_invoice"
+    STANDARD = "standard"
+    ESTIMATED = "estimated"
+    OVERRIDE = "override"
+    UNKNOWN = "unknown"
+
+
+@dataclass
+class CostResolution:
+    """Result of cost resolution."""
+    unit_cost: Decimal
+    cost_source: str
+    has_estimate: bool
+    estimate_reason: Optional[str] = None
+    lot_id: Optional[str] = None  # If resolved from a specific lot
+
+
+def resolve_cost_for_lot(
+    lot: InventoryLot,
+    product: Optional[Product] = None
+) -> CostResolution:
+    """
+    Resolve cost for a specific lot using cost resolution order:
+    1. FIFO actual from lot.current_unit_cost or lot.unit_cost
+    2. Standard cost from product
+    3. Estimated cost from product
+    
+    Args:
+        lot: Inventory lot to resolve cost for
+        product: Product (optional, will use lot.product if not provided)
+        
+    Returns:
+        CostResolution with unit cost, source, and estimate flags
+    """
+    product = product or lot.product
+    
+    # Priority 1: FIFO actual from lot
+    if lot.current_unit_cost is not None:
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(lot.current_unit_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.FIFO_ACTUAL.value,
+            has_estimate=False,
+            lot_id=lot.id
+        )
+    
+    if lot.unit_cost is not None:  # Legacy fallback
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(lot.unit_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.FIFO_ACTUAL.value,
+            has_estimate=False,
+            lot_id=lot.id
+        )
+    
+    # Priority 2: Standard cost
+    if product and product.standard_cost is not None:
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(product.standard_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.STANDARD.value,
+            has_estimate=False
+        )
+    
+    # Priority 3: Estimated cost
+    if product and product.estimated_cost is not None:
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(product.estimated_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.ESTIMATED.value,
+            has_estimate=True,
+            estimate_reason=product.estimate_reason
+        )
+    
+    # No cost available
+    return CostResolution(
+        unit_cost=Decimal("0"),
+        cost_source=CostSource.UNKNOWN.value,
+        has_estimate=False
+    )
+
+
+def resolve_cost_for_product(
+    product: Product,
+    lots: Optional[List[InventoryLot]] = None
+) -> CostResolution:
+    """
+    Resolve cost for a product using cost resolution order:
+    1. Average FIFO actual from available lots
+    2. Standard cost from product
+    3. Estimated cost from product
+    
+    Args:
+        product: Product to resolve cost for
+        lots: Optional list of lots for this product (if not provided, uses product.inventory_lots)
+        
+    Returns:
+        CostResolution with unit cost, source, and estimate flags
+    """
+    # Priority 1: FIFO actual from lots
+    if lots is None:
+        lots = [lot for lot in product.inventory_lots if lot.quantity_kg > 0 and lot.is_active]
+    
+    if lots:
+        # Use average of lots with actual costs
+        lots_with_costs = [
+            lot for lot in lots
+            if (lot.current_unit_cost is not None) or (lot.unit_cost is not None)
+        ]
+        
+        if lots_with_costs:
+            total_cost = Decimal("0")
+            total_qty = Decimal("0")
+            
+            for lot in lots_with_costs:
+                cost = lot.current_unit_cost or lot.unit_cost or Decimal("0")
+                if cost > 0:
+                    total_cost += cost * lot.quantity_kg
+                    total_qty += lot.quantity_kg
+            
+            if total_qty > 0:
+                avg_cost = total_cost / total_qty
+                return CostResolution(
+                    unit_cost=round_money(avg_cost),
+                    cost_source=CostSource.FIFO_ACTUAL.value,
+                    has_estimate=False
+                )
+    
+    # Priority 2: Standard cost
+    if product.standard_cost is not None:
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(product.standard_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.STANDARD.value,
+            has_estimate=False
+        )
+    
+    # Priority 3: Estimated cost
+    if product.estimated_cost is not None:
+        return CostResolution(
+            unit_cost=round_money(product.estimated_cost),
+            cost_source=CostSource.ESTIMATED.value,
+            has_estimate=True,
+            estimate_reason=product.estimate_reason
+        )
+    
+    # No cost available
+    return CostResolution(
+        unit_cost=Decimal("0"),
+        cost_source=CostSource.UNKNOWN.value,
+        has_estimate=False
+    )
+
+
+def get_item_cost(
+    product: Product,
+    as_of_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
+    lots: Optional[List[InventoryLot]] = None
+) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    """
+    Get cost information for an item with point-in-time support.
+    
+    Args:
+        product: Product to get cost for
+        as_of_date: Optional point-in-time date (for historical costing)
+        lots: Optional filtered list of lots (for point-in-time filtering)
+        
+    Returns:
+        Dictionary with unit_cost, cost_source, has_estimate, estimate_reason
+    """
+    cost_resolution = resolve_cost_for_product(product, lots)
+    
+    return {
+        'unit_cost': cost_resolution.unit_cost,
+        'cost_source': cost_resolution.cost_source,
+        'has_estimate': cost_resolution.has_estimate,
+        'estimate_reason': cost_resolution.estimate_reason
+    }
+
+
+def calculate_excise(
+    volume_l: Decimal,
+    abv_percent: Decimal,
+    excise_rate_per_l_abv: Decimal
+) -> Decimal:
+    """
+    Calculate excise payable based on ABV × volume × excise rate.
+    
+    Formula: excise = volume_L × (ABV / 100) × rate_per_L_ABV
+    
+    Args:
+        volume_l: Volume in liters
+        abv_percent: ABV as percentage (e.g., 40.0 for 40% v/v)
+        excise_rate_per_l_abv: Excise rate in $/L ABV
+        
+    Returns:
+        Excise amount in dollars (rounded to 2 decimal places)
+    """
+    if volume_l <= 0:
+        return Decimal("0")
+    if abv_percent <= 0:
+        return Decimal("0")
+    if excise_rate_per_l_abv <= 0:
+        return Decimal("0")
+    
+    # Calculate liters of ABV
+    liters_abv = volume_l * (abv_percent / Decimal("100"))
+    
+    # Calculate excise payable
+    excise = liters_abv * excise_rate_per_l_abv
+    
+    return round_money(excise)

         reservation.status = "RELEASED"

+    
+    def get_inventory_summary(self, product_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+        """
+        Get comprehensive inventory summary for a product including costs.
+        
+        Calculates:
+        - Stock on hand (kg)
+        - FIFO cost per kg (from oldest lot with quantity > 0)
+        - FIFO total value
+        - Average cost per kg (weighted average of all lots)
+        - Average total value
+        - Cost source and estimate flags
+        
+        Args:
+            product_id: Product ID
+            
+        Returns:
+            Dictionary with inventory summary fields:
+            - stock_on_hand_kg: Total quantity in kg
+            - fifo_cost_per_kg: Cost per kg from FIFO method
+            - fifo_total_value: Total value using FIFO cost
+            - average_cost_per_kg: Weighted average cost per kg
+            - average_total_value: Total value using average cost
+            - cost_source: Source of cost (fifo_actual, standard, estimated, etc.)
+            - has_estimate: Whether cost is estimated
+            - estimate_reason: Reason for estimate if applicable
+            - lots_count: Number of active lots
+        """
+        # Get all active lots ordered by FIFO (oldest first)
+        lots = self.get_lots_fifo(product_id)
+        
+        # Calculate stock on hand
+        stock_on_hand_kg = round_quantity(sum(lot.quantity_kg for lot in lots))
+        lots_count = len(lots)
+        
+        # Get product for cost resolution
+        product = self.db.get(Product, product_id)
+        if not product:
+            raise ValueError(f"Product {product_id} not found")
+        
+        # Calculate FIFO cost from oldest lot with quantity > 0
+        fifo_cost_per_kg = Decimal("0")
+        for lot in lots:
+            if lot.quantity_kg > 0:
+                # Use current_unit_cost, fallback to unit_cost, fallback to resolved cost
+                fifo_cost_per_kg = (
+                    lot.current_unit_cost or 
+                    lot.unit_cost or 
+                    Decimal("0")
+                )
+                if fifo_cost_per_kg == 0:
+                    # Resolve cost if lot doesn't have one
+                    cost_resolution = resolve_cost_for_lot(lot, product)
+                    fifo_cost_per_kg = cost_resolution.unit_cost
+                break
+        
+        # If no lots or no FIFO cost found, use CostingService fallback
+        if fifo_cost_per_kg == 0:
+            costing_service = CostingService(self.db)
+            try:
+                cost_info = costing_service.get_current_cost(product_id)
+                fifo_cost_per_kg = cost_info['unit_cost']
+            except Exception:
+                fifo_cost_per_kg = product.standard_cost or Decimal("0")
+        
+        fifo_cost_per_kg = round_money(fifo_cost_per_kg)
+        fifo_total_value = round_money(stock_on_hand_kg * fifo_cost_per_kg)
+        
+        # Calculate average cost (weighted average by quantity)
+        total_cost_value = Decimal("0")
+        total_quantity = Decimal("0")
+        
+        for lot in lots:
+            if lot.quantity_kg > 0:
+                lot_cost = (
+                    lot.current_unit_cost or 
+                    lot.unit_cost or 
+                    Decimal("0")
+                )
+                if lot_cost == 0:
+                    # Resolve cost if lot doesn't have one
+                    cost_resolution = resolve_cost_for_lot(lot, product)
+                    lot_cost = cost_resolution.unit_cost
+                
+                total_cost_value += lot.quantity_kg * lot_cost
+                total_quantity += lot.quantity_kg
+        
+        average_cost_per_kg = Decimal("0")
+        if total_quantity > 0:
+            average_cost_per_kg = round_money(total_cost_value / total_quantity)
+        
+        average_total_value = round_money(stock_on_hand_kg * average_cost_per_kg)
+        
+        # Get cost source and estimate flags from CostingService
+        costing_service = CostingService(self.db)
+        try:
+            cost_info = costing_service.get_current_cost(product_id)
+            cost_source = cost_info.get('cost_source', CostSource.STANDARD.value)
+            has_estimate = cost_info.get('has_estimate', False)
+            estimate_reason = cost_info.get('estimate_reason')
+        except Exception:
+            cost_source = CostSource.STANDARD.value
+            has_estimate = False
+            estimate_reason = None
+        
+        return {
+            'stock_on_hand_kg': float(stock_on_hand_kg),
+            'fifo_cost_per_kg': float(fifo_cost_per_kg),
+            'fifo_total_value': float(fifo_total_value),
+            'average_cost_per_kg': float(average_cost_per_kg),
+            'average_total_value': float(average_total_value),
+            'cost_source': cost_source,
+            'has_estimate': has_estimate,
+            'estimate_reason': estimate_reason,
+            'lots_count': lots_count
+        }

+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("contact-detail-title", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-code", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-name", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-person", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-active", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-email", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-phone", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-address", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-customer", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-supplier", "children"),
+         Output("contact-detail-other", "children")],
+        [Input("contacts-table", "selected_rows")],
+        [State("contacts-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=False
+    )
+    def update_contact_detail(selected_rows, data):
+        """Update contact detail pane when row is selected."""
+        if not selected_rows or not data or len(selected_rows) == 0:
+            return (
+                "Select a contact...",
+                "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-"
+            )
+        
+        contact = data[selected_rows[0]]
+        
+        # Helper to format boolean values
+        def format_bool(value):
+            if isinstance(value, bool):
+                return "Yes" if value else "No"
+            if isinstance(value, str):
+                return "Yes" if value.lower() in ("true", "1", "yes", "y") else "No"
+            return "No" if not value else "Yes"
+        
+        return (
+            contact.get("name") or "Unknown Contact",
+            contact.get("code") or "-",
+            contact.get("name") or "-",
+            contact.get("contact_person") or "-",
+            format_bool(contact.get("is_active")),
+            contact.get("email") or "-",
+            contact.get("phone") or "-",
+            contact.get("address") or "-",
+            format_bool(contact.get("is_customer")),
+            format_bool(contact.get("is_supplier")),
+            format_bool(contact.get("is_other"))
+        )

+    def normalize_unit(unit_str):
+        """Normalize unit string to domain rules format (uppercase, L not LT)."""
+        if not unit_str:
+            return "KG"
+        unit_upper = str(unit_str).upper()
+        # Map common variations
+        unit_map = {
+            "LT": "L",
+            "LITRE": "L",
+            "LITER": "L",
+            "LITERS": "L",
+            "LITRES": "L",
+        }
+        return unit_map.get(unit_upper, unit_upper)

+    # Calculate live values for formula editor lines
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("formula-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("formula-editor-total-lines", "children"),
+         Output("formula-editor-total-kg", "children"),
+         Output("formula-editor-total-l", "children"),
+         Output("formula-editor-total-sg", "children"),
+         Output("formula-editor-total-cost", "children")],
+        [Input("formula-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def calculate_formula_values(lines_data):
+        """Calculate kg, L, cost and totals for each line, and overall totals."""
+        try:
+            if not lines_data or not isinstance(lines_data, list):
+                return [], "0", "0.000 kg", "0.000 L", "-", "$0.00"
+            
+            # Create a copy to avoid mutating the original
+            import copy
+            updated_lines = copy.deepcopy(lines_data)
+            
+            total_kg = Decimal("0")
+            total_l = Decimal("0")
+            total_cost = Decimal("0")
+            
+            # Process each line
+            for line in updated_lines:
+                if not isinstance(line, dict):
+                    continue
+                    
+                quantity_str = line.get("quantity", "0")
+                unit = line.get("unit", "kg")
+                density = line.get("density_kg_per_l")
+                unit_cost = line.get("unit_cost")
+                
+                try:
+                    quantity = Decimal(str(quantity_str))
+                except:
+                    quantity = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Convert to kg using domain rules
+                kg_value = Decimal("0")
+                if quantity > 0:
+                    try:
+                        density_dec = Decimal(str(density)) if density is not None else None
+                        normalized_unit = normalize_unit(unit)
+                        result = to_kg(quantity, normalized_unit, density_dec)
+                        kg_value = result.quantity_kg
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"Conversion error for {quantity} {unit}: {e}")
+                        kg_value = quantity  # Fallback
+                
+                # Calculate L from kg using density
+                l_value = Decimal("0")
+                if density is not None and density > 0 and kg_value > 0:
+                    try:
+                        density_dec = Decimal(str(density))
+                        l_value = to_liters(kg_value, density_dec, "L")
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"L conversion error: {e}")
+                        l_value = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Calculate line cost
+                line_cost = Decimal("0")
+                if unit_cost is not None and kg_value > 0:
+                    try:
+                        unit_cost_dec = Decimal(str(unit_cost))
+                        line_cost = round_money(unit_cost_dec * kg_value)
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"Cost calculation error: {e}")
+                        line_cost = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Update line with calculated values
+                line["quantity_kg_display"] = float(kg_value)
+                line["quantity_l_display"] = float(l_value) if l_value > 0 else 0.0
+                line["unit_cost_display"] = float(unit_cost) if unit_cost is not None else 0.0
+                line["line_cost_display"] = float(line_cost)
+                
+                # Add to totals
+                total_kg += kg_value
+                if l_value > 0:
+                    total_l += l_value
+                total_cost += line_cost
+            
+            # Calculate recipe SG
+            recipe_sg = Decimal("0")
+            if total_l > 0:
+                recipe_sg = total_kg / total_l
+            
+            total_cost_rounded = round_money(total_cost)
+            
+            return (
+                updated_lines,
+                str(len(updated_lines)),
+                f"{float(total_kg):.3f} kg",
+                f"{float(total_l):.3f} L" if float(total_l) > 0 else "-",
+                f"{float(recipe_sg):.6f}" if float(recipe_sg) > 0 else "-",
+                f"${float(total_cost_rounded):.2f}"
+            )
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error in calculate_formula_values: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return [], "0", "0.000 kg", "0.000 L", "-", "$0.00"
+

+        def safe_format(value, format_type="text"):
+            if value is None or value == "":
+                return "-"
+            if format_type == "currency":
+                try:
+                    return f"${float(value):.2f}"
+                except:
+                    return str(value)
+            elif format_type == "decimal":
+                try:
+                    return f"{float(value):.3f}"
+                except:
+                    return str(value)
+            elif format_type == "percent":
+                try:
+                    return f"{float(value):.2f}%"
+                except:
+                    return str(value)
+            elif format_type == "boolean":
+                if isinstance(value, bool):
+                    return "Yes" if value else "No"
+                if isinstance(value, str):
+                    return "Yes" if value.lower() in ("true", "1", "yes", "y") else "No"
+                return str(value)
+            return str(value)

+        # Build cost pricing table with new columns
+        # Calculate values for each cost type row
+        def calculate_cost_pricing_row(cost_ex_gst_val, excise_val, distributor_inc_gst_val, retail_inc_gst_val):
+            """Calculate all derived values for a cost pricing row."""
+            # Ex-GST + Excise
+            ex_gst_plus_excise = cost_ex_gst_val + excise_val
+            
+            # Excised = (ex-GST + excise) * 1.1
+            excised = ex_gst_plus_excise * 1.1
+            
+            # UnExcised = ex-GST * 1.1
+            unexcised = cost_ex_gst_val * 1.1
+            
+            # Profit margin from cost to distributor (as percentage)
+            profit_margin_cost = 0.0
+            if cost_ex_gst_val > 0 and distributor_inc_gst_val > 0:
+                # Convert distributor inc GST to ex GST for comparison
+                distributor_ex_gst = distributor_inc_gst_val / 1.1
+                profit_margin_cost = ((distributor_ex_gst - cost_ex_gst_val) / cost_ex_gst_val) * 100
+            
+            # Profit margin between distributor and retail (as percentage)
+            profit_margin_dist_retail = 0.0
+            if distributor_inc_gst_val > 0 and retail_inc_gst_val > 0:
+                distributor_ex_gst = distributor_inc_gst_val / 1.1
+                retail_ex_gst = retail_inc_gst_val / 1.1
+                profit_margin_dist_retail = ((retail_ex_gst - distributor_ex_gst) / distributor_ex_gst) * 100
+            
+            return {
+                "ex_gst_plus_excise": safe_format(ex_gst_plus_excise, "currency"),
+                "excised": safe_format(excised, "currency"),
+                "unexcised": safe_format(unexcised, "currency"),
+                "profit_margin_cost": safe_format(profit_margin_cost, "percent"),
+                "profit_margin_dist_retail": safe_format(profit_margin_dist_retail, "percent"),
+            }
+        
+        # Get excise value (excise is stored per price level, use distributor excise)
