+                "profit_margin_dist_retail": purchase_row["profit_margin_dist_retail"],
+            },
+            {
+                "cost_type": "Usage Cost",
+                "ex_gst": safe_format(usage_cost_ex_gst, "currency"),
+                "excise": safe_format(excise_value, "currency"),
+                "ex_gst_plus_excise": usage_row["ex_gst_plus_excise"],
+                "excised": usage_row["excised"],
+                "unexcised": usage_row["unexcised"],
+                "distributor_inc_gst": safe_format(distributor_price_inc_gst, "currency"),
+                "profit_margin_cost": usage_row["profit_margin_cost"],
+                "retail_inc_gst": safe_format(retail_price_inc_gst, "currency"),
+                "profit_margin_dist_retail": usage_row["profit_margin_dist_retail"],
+            },
+        ]
+        
+        pricing_table = dash_table.DataTable(
+            data=pricing_data,
+            columns=pricing_columns,
+            id="detail-pricing-table",
+            editable=False,
+            style_cell={'textAlign': 'left', 'padding': '5px', 'fontSize': '12px'},
+            style_header={'backgroundColor': 'rgb(230, 230, 230)', 'fontWeight': 'bold', 'fontSize': '11px'},
+            style_data={'fontSize': '11px', 'whiteSpace': 'pre-wrap'},
+        )
+        
+        cost_table = dash_table.DataTable(
+            data=cost_data,
+            columns=cost_columns,
+            id="detail-cost-table",
+            editable=False,
+            style_cell={'textAlign': 'left', 'padding': '5px', 'fontSize': '12px'},
+            style_header={'backgroundColor': 'rgb(230, 230, 230)', 'fontWeight': 'bold', 'fontSize': '11px'},
+            style_data={'fontSize': '11px', 'whiteSpace': 'pre-wrap'},
+        )
+        
+        # Format capabilities for display
+        capabilities = []
+        if product.get("is_purchase", False):
+            capabilities.append("Purchase")
+        if product.get("is_sell", False):
+            capabilities.append("Sell")
+        if product.get("is_assemble", False):
+            capabilities.append("Assemble")
+        capabilities_str = ", ".join(capabilities) if capabilities else "None"
+        
+        return (
+            product.get("name") or "Unknown Product",  # title
+            product.get("sku") or "-",  # sku
+            capabilities_str,  # capabilities
+            product.get("name") or "-",  # name
+            product.get("description") or "-",  # description
+            product.get("base_unit") or "-",  # base_unit
+            product.get("size") or "-",  # size
+            safe_format(product.get("density_kg_per_l"), "decimal"),  # density
+            safe_format(product.get("abv_percent"), "percent"),  # abv
+            pricing_table,  # pricing_table
+            consolidated_table,  # consolidated_table
+            cost_table,  # cost_table
+            safe_format(product.get("restock_level"), "decimal"),  # restock
+            safe_format(product.get("is_active"), "boolean")  # active
+        )
+    
     # Note: Table refresh is now handled by the main callback in app.py that responds to filter changes
+    
+    # Auto-calculate excise and GST for pricing tables
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("product-pricing-table", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+        [Input("product-pricing-table", "data"),
+         Input("product-abv", "value"),
+         Input("product-density", "value"),
+         Input("product-size", "value"),
+         Input("product-base-unit", "value")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def calculate_pricing_excise_and_gst(pricing_data, abv, density, size, base_unit):
+        """Calculate excise and GST based on entered prices, ABV, and volume."""
+        if not pricing_data:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        # Only trigger if pricing table data changed
+        trigger_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        if trigger_id != "product-pricing-table":
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        # Need ABV and volume to calculate excise
+        if not abv or not size:
+            return pricing_data
+        
+        try:
+            # Get product volume and convert to liters based on base_unit
+            volume = float(size) if size else 0
+            abv_pct = float(abv) if abv else 0
+            try:
+                density_val = float(density) if density else None
+            except (ValueError, TypeError):
+                density_val = None
+            base_unit_str = str(base_unit).upper() if base_unit else ""
+            
+            # Convert volume to liters based on base_unit
+            volume_l = volume  # Default assume liters
+            if base_unit_str == "ML" or base_unit_str == "MILLILITER" or base_unit_str == "MILLILITRE":
+                volume_l = volume * 0.001  # Convert ml to L
+            elif base_unit_str == "KG" or base_unit_str == "KILOGRAM":
+                # For mass units, need density to convert to liters
+                if density_val and density_val > 0:
+                    volume_l = volume / density_val  # kg / (kg/L) = L
+                else:
+                    # Can't calculate excise without density
+                    print(f"Warning: Cannot calculate excise for {base_unit_str} without density")
+                    return pricing_data
+            elif base_unit_str in ["L", "LITRE", "LITER", "LT"]:
+                volume_l = volume  # Already in liters
+            # else: assume it's already in liters (legacy behavior)
+            
+            # Get current excise rate from API (most recent rate active today)
+            excise_rate = 99.52  # Default Australian rate
+            try:
+                excise_rates = make_api_request("GET", "/excise-rates/")
+                if excise_rates and isinstance(excise_rates, list):
+                    # Get the most recent rate (assuming they're ordered by date)
+                    for rate in excise_rates:
+                        rate_value = rate.get("rate_per_l_abv")
+                        if rate_value:
+                            excise_rate = float(rate_value)
+                            break
+            except Exception:
+                pass  # Use default
+            
+            # Calculate excise per unit for this product
+            # Excise = volume_L × (ABV%) × excise_rate($/L ABV)
+            liters_abv = volume_l * (abv_pct / 100.0)
+            excise_per_unit = liters_abv * excise_rate
+            
+            # Deep copy the data to avoid mutating the original
+            updated_data = []
+            for row in pricing_data:
+                updated_row = dict(row)  # Create a new dict for each row
+                updated_data.append(updated_row)
+            
+            # Update each price level
+            for row in updated_data:
+                inc_gst_val = row.get("inc_gst")
+                ex_gst_val = row.get("ex_gst")
+                excise_val = row.get("excise")
+                
+                # Auto-calculate excise if not set and we have ABV
+                if not excise_val or excise_val == "" or excise_val is None:
+                    row["excise"] = round(excise_per_unit, 2)
+                
+                # Auto-calculate Inc GST or Ex GST based on the other
+                if inc_gst_val and inc_gst_val != "":
+                    # Inc GST was entered, calculate Ex GST
+                    ex_gst_calc = float(inc_gst_val) / 1.10
+                    if not ex_gst_val or ex_gst_val == "":
+                        row["ex_gst"] = round(ex_gst_calc, 2)
+                elif ex_gst_val and ex_gst_val != "":
+                    # Ex GST was entered, calculate Inc GST
+                    inc_gst_calc = float(ex_gst_val) * 1.10
+                    if not inc_gst_val or inc_gst_val == "":
+                        row["inc_gst"] = round(inc_gst_calc, 2)
+            
+            return updated_data
+        except (ValueError, TypeError) as e:
+            print(f"Error calculating pricing: {e}")
+            return pricing_data
+    
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("product-cost-table", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+        [Input("product-cost-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def calculate_cost_gst(cost_data):
+        """Calculate GST for cost table based on entered prices and tax_included flag.
+        
+        Only auto-calculates the OTHER field when the target field is empty.
+        This allows users to edit/delete either field independently.
+        """
+        if not cost_data:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        trigger_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        if trigger_id != "product-cost-table":
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        try:
+            # Deep copy the data to avoid mutating the original
+            updated_data = []
+            for row in cost_data:
+                updated_row = dict(row)  # Create a new dict for each row
+                updated_data.append(updated_row)
+            
+            # Update cost rows based on tax_included flag
+            # Only auto-calculate if the target field is empty/None
+            for row in updated_data:
+                inc_gst_val = row.get("inc_gst")
+                ex_gst_val = row.get("ex_gst")
+                tax_included = row.get("tax_included", "N")
+                
+                # Normalize empty values (None, "", "None", 0)
+                def is_empty(val):
+                    return val is None or val == "" or val == "None" or (isinstance(val, (int, float)) and val == 0)
+                
+                inc_empty = is_empty(inc_gst_val)
+                ex_empty = is_empty(ex_gst_val)
+                
+                # If tax is not included, Inc GST and Ex GST should be the same
+                if tax_included == "N":
+                    # When tax not included, both should match
+                    if not ex_empty and inc_empty:
+                        # ex_gst has value, copy to inc_gst
+                        try:
+                            row["inc_gst"] = float(ex_gst_val)
+                        except (ValueError, TypeError):
+                            pass
+                    elif not inc_empty and ex_empty:
+                        # inc_gst has value, copy to ex_gst
+                        try:
+                            row["ex_gst"] = float(inc_gst_val)
+                        except (ValueError, TypeError):
+                            pass
+                    elif not inc_empty and not ex_empty:
+                        # Both have values - keep both (user can edit either independently)
+                        pass
+                else:
+                    # Tax included: Auto-calculate ONLY if the target field is empty
+                    if not inc_empty and ex_empty:
+                        # Inc GST was entered and ex_gst is empty, calculate Ex GST
+                        try:
+                            ex_gst_calc = float(inc_gst_val) / 1.10
+                            row["ex_gst"] = round(ex_gst_calc, 2)
+                        except (ValueError, TypeError):
+                            pass
+                    elif not ex_empty and inc_empty:
+                        # Ex GST was entered and inc_gst is empty, calculate Inc GST
+                        try:
+                            inc_gst_calc = float(ex_gst_val) * 1.10
+                            row["inc_gst"] = round(inc_gst_calc, 2)
+                        except (ValueError, TypeError):
+                            pass
+                    # If both have values or both are empty, don't auto-calculate
+                    # This allows user to edit/delete either field independently
+            
+            return updated_data
+        except (ValueError, TypeError) as e:
+            print(f"Error calculating cost GST: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return cost_data
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Unexpected error in calculate_cost_gst: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return cost_data
+    
+    # Old assembly definition callbacks removed - replaced with assembly lines CRUD above
+    
+    # Update product detail pane with inventory data
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("product-detail-stock", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-lots-count", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-fifo-cost", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-fifo-value", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-avg-cost", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-cost-source", "children"),
+         Output("product-detail-has-estimate", "children")],
+        [Input("products-table", "selected_rows")],
+        [State("products-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=False
+    )
+    def update_product_inventory_detail(selected_rows, data):
+        """Update inventory section in product detail pane."""
+        if not selected_rows or not data or len(selected_rows) == 0:
+            return ("-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-")
+        
+        product = data[selected_rows[0]]
+        inventory = product.get("inventory")
+        
+        if not inventory:
+            return ("-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-", "-")
+        
+        def safe_format(value, format_type="text"):
+            if value is None:
+                return "-"
+            if format_type == "currency":
+                try:
+                    return f"${float(value):.2f}"
+                except:
+                    return str(value)
+            elif format_type == "decimal":
+                try:
+                    return f"{float(value):.3f}"
+                except:
+                    return str(value)
+            return str(value)
+        
+        return (
+            safe_format(inventory.get("stock_on_hand_kg"), "decimal"),
+            str(inventory.get("lots_count", 0)),
+            safe_format(inventory.get("fifo_cost_per_kg"), "currency"),
+            safe_format(inventory.get("fifo_total_value"), "currency"),
+            safe_format(inventory.get("average_cost_per_kg"), "currency"),
+            inventory.get("cost_source", "-") or "-",
+            "Yes" if inventory.get("has_estimate") else "No"
+        )
+    
+    # Update primary assembly info in product detail pane
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("product-detail-primary-assembly", "children"),
+        [Input("products-table", "selected_rows")],
+        [State("products-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=False
+    )
+    def update_product_primary_assembly(selected_rows, data):
+        """Display primary assembly information for products with is_assemble=True."""
+        if not selected_rows or not data or len(selected_rows) == 0:
+            return html.Div()
+        
+        product = data[selected_rows[0]]
+        is_assemble = product.get("is_assemble", False)
+        product_id = product.get("id")
+        
+        # Only show for products that can be assembled
+        if not is_assemble or not product_id:
+            return html.Div()
+        
+        try:
+            # Fetch assemblies for this product with timeout
+            try:
+                assemblies_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={product_id}", timeout=5)
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"Error fetching assemblies: {e}")
+                return html.Div([
+                    html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                    html.P("Error loading assemblies.", className="text-danger")
+                ])
+            
+            assemblies = []
+            if isinstance(assemblies_response, list):
+                assemblies = assemblies_response
+            elif isinstance(assemblies_response, dict):
+                if "error" in assemblies_response:
+                    return html.Div([
+                        html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                        html.P("Error loading assemblies.", className="text-danger")
+                    ])
+                elif "assemblies" in assemblies_response:
+                    assemblies = assemblies_response.get("assemblies", [])
+            
+            # Find primary assembly
+            primary_assembly = None
+            for assembly in assemblies:
+                if assembly.get("is_primary", False) and assembly.get("is_active", True):
+                    primary_assembly = assembly
+                    break
+            
+            if not primary_assembly:
+                return html.Div([
+                    html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                    html.P("No primary assembly defined.", className="text-muted")
+                ])
+            
+            # Get full assembly details with lines (with timeout)
+            assembly_id = primary_assembly.get("id")
+            try:
+                assembly_details = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/{assembly_id}", timeout=5)
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"Error fetching assembly details: {e}")
+                return html.Div([
+                    html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                    html.P("Error loading assembly details.", className="text-danger")
+                ])
+            
+            if isinstance(assembly_details, dict) and "error" in assembly_details:
+                return html.Div([
+                    html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                    html.P("Error loading assembly details.", className="text-danger")
+                ])
+            
+            lines = assembly_details.get("lines", [])
+            
+            # Limit number of lines to process to avoid timeout (show first 20)
+            lines_to_process = lines[:20]
+            if len(lines) > 20:
+                print(f"Warning: Primary assembly has {len(lines)} lines, showing first 20 only")
+            
+            # Build assembly lines table
+            # Skip individual product lookups to avoid timeout - use data from assembly response if available
+            lines_data = []
+            total_cost = 0.0
+            for idx, line in enumerate(lines_to_process):
+                component_product_id = line.get("component_product_id", "")
+                quantity_kg = float(line.get("quantity", 0))
+                unit = line.get("unit", "kg")
+                
+                # Try to get component info from line data first (if API returns it)
+                component_name = line.get("component_name") or line.get("component_product_name") or f"Product {component_product_id[:8]}..." if component_product_id else "Unknown"
+                unit_cost = line.get("unit_cost") or line.get("usage_cost_ex_gst") or line.get("usage_cost_inc_gst")
+                
+                # Only fetch product details if we don't have proper name/cost and component_id exists
+                # Limit to avoid timeout - only fetch for first 5 lines that need it
+                needs_lookup = (component_name.startswith("Product ") or not component_name or component_name == "Unknown") and component_product_id
+                if needs_lookup and idx < 5:
+                    if component_product_id:
+                        try:
+                            # Use shorter timeout for individual product lookups
+                            component_product = make_api_request("GET", f"/products/{component_product_id}", timeout=2)
+                            if isinstance(component_product, dict) and "error" not in component_product:
+                                sku = component_product.get("sku", "")
+                                name = component_product.get("name", "")
+                                if sku or name:
+                                    component_name = f"{sku} - {name}" if sku else name
+                                if not unit_cost:
+                                    unit_cost = component_product.get("usage_cost_ex_gst") or component_product.get("usage_cost_inc_gst")
+                        except Exception as e:
+                            # If lookup fails, continue with existing data
+                            print(f"Warning: Could not fetch product {component_product_id}: {e}")
+                            pass
+                
+                line_cost = (float(unit_cost) * quantity_kg) if unit_cost else 0.0
+                total_cost += line_cost
+                
+                lines_data.append({
+                    "Component": component_name,
+                    "Quantity": f"{quantity_kg:.3f}",
+                    "Unit": unit,
+                    "Cost": f"${line_cost:.2f}" if line_cost > 0 else "-"
+                })
+            
+            assembly_table = dash_table.DataTable(
+                data=lines_data,
+                columns=[
+                    {"name": "Component", "id": "Component"},
+                    {"name": "Quantity", "id": "Quantity"},
+                    {"name": "Unit", "id": "Unit"},
+                    {"name": "Cost", "id": "Cost"},
+                ],
+                id="detail-primary-assembly-table",
+                editable=False,
+                style_cell={'textAlign': 'left', 'padding': '5px', 'fontSize': '12px'},
+                style_header={'backgroundColor': 'rgb(230, 230, 230)', 'fontWeight': 'bold', 'fontSize': '11px'},
+                style_data={'fontSize': '11px'},
+            )
+            
+            return html.Div([
+                html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                html.P([
+                    html.Strong("Name: "),
+                    primary_assembly.get("assembly_name", "Unknown"),
+                    html.Br(),
+                    html.Strong("Version: "),
+                    str(primary_assembly.get("version", 1)),
+                    html.Br(),
+                    html.Strong("Total Cost: "),
+                    f"${total_cost:.2f}"
+                ], className="mb-2"),
+                assembly_table,
+                html.P(f"Showing {len(lines_to_process)} of {len(lines)} lines", className="text-muted text-small mt-2") if len(lines) > 20 else html.Div()
+            ])
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error loading primary assembly: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return html.Div([
+                html.H6("Primary Assembly"),
+                html.P(f"Error loading assembly: {str(e)}", className="text-danger")
+            ])
+    
+    # Open inventory adjustment modal
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("inventory-adjustment-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-product-id-hidden", "children", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-quantity", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-lot", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-unit-cost", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-notes", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-reference-type", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("adjustment-reference-id", "value", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("adjust-inventory-btn", "n_clicks"),
+         Input("adjustment-cancel-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("products-table", "selected_rows"),
+         State("products-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def open_inventory_adjustment_modal(open_clicks, cancel_clicks, selected_rows, data):
+        """Open inventory adjustment modal and populate product ID."""
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        button_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        
+        if button_id == "adjustment-cancel-btn":
+            return False, "", None, None, None, "", "MANUAL", ""
+        
+        if button_id == "adjust-inventory-btn":
+            if not selected_rows or not data:
+                return no_update, "", None, None, None, "", "MANUAL", ""
+            
+            product = data[selected_rows[0]]
+            product_id = product.get("id")
+            
+            # Load lots for this product
+            try:
+                lots_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/inventory/product/{product_id}/summary")
+                # We can't load individual lots yet, but we can prepare for it
+                lot_options = []
+            except Exception:
+                lot_options = []
+            
+            return (
+                True,  # is_open
+                str(product_id),  # product_id
+                None,  # quantity
+                None,  # lot_id
+                None,  # unit_cost
+                "",  # notes
+                "MANUAL",  # reference_type
+                ""  # reference_id
+            )
+        
+        raise PreventUpdate
+    
+    # Submit inventory adjustment
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("inventory-adjustment-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "header", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "children", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("products-refresh", "n_clicks", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("adjustment-submit-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("adjustment-product-id-hidden", "children"),
+         State("adjustment-type", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-quantity", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-lot", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-unit-cost", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-notes", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-reference-type", "value"),
+         State("adjustment-reference-id", "value"),
+         State("products-refresh", "n_clicks")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def submit_inventory_adjustment(
+        n_clicks, product_id, adjustment_type, quantity, lot_id, unit_cost, notes, 
+        reference_type, reference_id, current_refresh_clicks
+    ):
+        """Submit inventory adjustment."""
+        if not n_clicks:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        # Validation
+        if not product_id or not adjustment_type or quantity is None or not notes:
+            return (True, True, "Error", "Product ID, adjustment type, quantity, and notes are required", no_update)
+        
+        try:
+            adjustment_data = {
+                "product_id": str(product_id),
+                "adjustment_type": adjustment_type,
+                "quantity_kg": float(quantity),
+                "notes": notes,
+            }
+            
+            if lot_id:
+                adjustment_data["lot_id"] = str(lot_id)
+            if unit_cost:
+                adjustment_data["unit_cost"] = float(unit_cost)
+            if reference_type:
+                adjustment_data["reference_type"] = reference_type
+            if reference_id:
+                adjustment_data["reference_id"] = str(reference_id)
+            
+            response = make_api_request("POST", "/inventory/adjust", adjustment_data)
+            
+            if isinstance(response, dict) and "error" in response:
+                return (True, True, "Error", response["error"], no_update)
+            
+            # Success - refresh products table
+            new_refresh_clicks = (current_refresh_clicks or 0) + 1
+            return (
+                False,  # Close modal
+                True,  # Show toast
+                "Success",
+                f"Inventory adjusted successfully",
+                new_refresh_clicks  # Refresh table
+            )
+        
+        except Exception as e:
+            return (True, True, "Error", f"Failed to adjust inventory: {str(e)}", no_update)
+    
+    # Conditional greying of sections based on product type flags
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("pricing-section-content", "style"),
+         Output("purchase-section-content", "style"),
+         Output("assembly-section-content", "style"),
+         Output("cost-settings-section-content", "style"),
+         Output("product-cost-table", "style_data_conditional", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("product-is-purchase", "value"),
+         Input("product-is-sell", "value"),
+         Input("product-is-assemble", "value")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def grey_out_sections(is_purchase, is_sell, is_assemble):
+        """Grey out sections based on product type flags."""
+        # Grey out pricing section if is_sell is False
+        pricing_style = {"pointerEvents": "none", "opacity": "0.5"} if not is_sell else {}
+        
+        # Grey out purchase section if is_purchase is False
+        purchase_style = {"pointerEvents": "none", "opacity": "0.5"} if not is_purchase else {}
+        
+        # Grey out assembly section if is_assemble is False
+        assembly_style = {"pointerEvents": "none", "opacity": "0.5"} if not is_assemble else {}
+        
+        # Cost settings is always visible but can grey out specific rows
+        cost_settings_style = {}
+        
+        # Conditional formatting for cost table rows
+        style_data_conditional = []
+        
+        # Grey out Purchase Cost row if is_purchase is False
+        # Use quotes for values with spaces in filter_query
+        if not is_purchase:
+            style_data_conditional.append({
+                "if": {"filter_query": '{cost_type} = "Purchase Cost"'},
+                "backgroundColor": "#f0f0f0",
+                "color": "#999"
+            })
+        
+        # Grey out Manufactured Cost row if is_assemble is False
+        if not is_assemble:
+            style_data_conditional.append({
+                "if": {"filter_query": '{cost_type} = "Manufactured Cost"'},
+                "backgroundColor": "#f0f0f0",
+                "color": "#999"
+            })
+        
+        return pricing_style, purchase_style, assembly_style, cost_settings_style, style_data_conditional
+    
+    # ========== ASSEMBLY CRUD CALLBACKS ==========
+    
+    # Helper function to format assemblies for table
+    def format_assemblies_for_table(assemblies):
+        """Format assembly list for DataTable, removing nested fields."""
+        table_data = []
+        for assembly in assemblies:
+            if not isinstance(assembly, dict):
+                continue
+            # Only include columns that exist in the table definition
+            row = {
+                "id": assembly.get("id", ""),
+                "assembly_code": assembly.get("assembly_code", ""),
+                "assembly_name": assembly.get("assembly_name", ""),
+                "version": assembly.get("version", 1),
+                "is_primary": "✓" if assembly.get("is_primary") else "",
+                "is_active": "✓" if assembly.get("is_active") else "",
+                "yield_factor": assembly.get("yield_factor", 1.0),
+                "total_cost": assembly.get("total_cost", 0.0),
+            }
+            table_data.append(row)
+        return table_data
+    
+    # Toggle assembly buttons based on selection
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("edit-assembly-btn", "disabled"),
+         Output("duplicate-assembly-btn", "disabled"),
+         Output("set-primary-assembly-btn", "disabled"),
+         Output("archive-assembly-btn", "disabled")],
+        Input("product-assemblies-table", "selected_rows"),
+        prevent_initial_call=False
+    )
+    def toggle_assembly_buttons(selected_rows):
+        """Enable/disable edit, duplicate, set primary, and archive buttons based on selection."""
+        disabled = not selected_rows or len(selected_rows) == 0
+        return disabled, disabled, disabled, disabled
+    
+    # Load assemblies for selected product
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("product-assemblies-table", "data"),
+        [Input("product-form-modal", "is_open"),
+         Input("product-form-hidden", "children")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def load_product_assemblies(modal_is_open, product_id_hidden):
+        """Load assemblies for the product when modal opens."""
+        if not modal_is_open:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        if not product_id_hidden or not product_id_hidden.strip():
+            return []
+        
+        product_id = product_id_hidden.strip()
+        
+        try:
+            # TODO: Add API endpoint to get assemblies for a product
+            # For now, return empty list
+            response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={product_id}")
+            if isinstance(response, dict) and "error" in response:
+                return []
+            
+            assemblies = response if isinstance(response, list) else []
+            
+            # Format for table display
+            return format_assemblies_for_table(assemblies)
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error loading assemblies: {e}")
+            return []
+    
+    # Open assembly editor modal for New/Edit/Duplicate
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-editor-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-editor-title", "children", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-input-version", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-input-name", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-input-active", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-input-notes", "value", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-form-hidden", "children", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-parent-product-id-hidden", "children", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("new-assembly-btn", "n_clicks"),
+         Input("edit-assembly-btn", "n_clicks"),
+         Input("duplicate-assembly-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("product-assemblies-table", "selected_rows"),
+         State("product-assemblies-table", "data"),
+         State("product-form-hidden", "children")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def open_assembly_editor(new_clicks, edit_clicks, duplicate_clicks, selected_rows, assemblies_data, product_id_hidden):
+        """Open assembly editor modal for new, edit, or duplicate."""
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        button_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        product_id = product_id_hidden.strip() if product_id_hidden else None
+        
+        if button_id == "new-assembly-btn":
+            # New assembly - clear form
+            if not product_id:
+                raise PreventUpdate
+            return (
+                True,  # is_open
+                "New Assembly",  # title
+                1,  # version
+                "",  # name
+                True,  # active
+                "",  # notes
+                [],  # lines
+                "",  # assembly_id (empty for new)
+                product_id  # parent_product_id
+            )
+        elif button_id in ("edit-assembly-btn", "duplicate-assembly-btn"):
+            # Edit or duplicate - populate with selected data
+            if not selected_rows or not assemblies_data:
+                raise PreventUpdate
+            
+            assembly = assemblies_data[selected_rows[0]]
+            
+            if button_id == "duplicate-assembly-btn":
+                # Duplicate - modify name and clear ID
+                title = "Duplicate Assembly"
+                assembly_name = f"{assembly.get('assembly_name', '')} (copy)"
+                assembly_id = ""
+            else:
+                # Edit
+                title = "Edit Assembly"
+                assembly_name = assembly.get("assembly_name", "")
+                assembly_id = str(assembly.get("id", ""))
+            
+            # Load assembly lines from API
+            lines_data = []
+            if assembly_id:
+                try:
+                    assembly_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/{assembly_id}")
+                    if not isinstance(assembly_response, dict) or "error" not in assembly_response:
+                        lines = assembly_response.get("lines", [])
+                        from app.domain.rules import convert_units
+                        from decimal import Decimal
+                        
+                        for line in lines:
+                            qty_kg = float(line.get("quantity", 0))
+                            unit = line.get("unit", "kg")
+                            
+                            # Convert from kg to display unit
+                            display_qty = qty_kg
+                            if unit and unit.upper() != "KG":
+                                try:
+                                    component_product = make_api_request("GET", f"/products/{line.get('component_product_id', '')}")
+                                    density = component_product.get("density_kg_per_l") if isinstance(component_product, dict) else None
+                                    density_dec = Decimal(str(density)) if density else None
+                                    normalized_unit = normalize_unit_assembly(unit)
+                                    result = convert_units(Decimal(str(qty_kg)), "KG", normalized_unit, density_dec)
+                                    display_qty = float(result.converted_quantity)
+                                except:
+                                    display_qty = qty_kg
+                            
+                            component_product = make_api_request("GET", f"/products/{line.get('component_product_id', '')}")
+                            component_name = ""
+                            density = None
+                            unit_cost = None
+                            base_unit = "kg"
+                            if isinstance(component_product, dict):
+                                sku = component_product.get("sku", "")
+                                name = component_product.get("name", "")
+                                component_name = f"{sku} - {name}"
+                                density = component_product.get("density_kg_per_l")
+                                unit_cost = component_product.get("usage_cost_ex_gst") or component_product.get("usage_cost_inc_gst")
+                                base_unit = component_product.get("base_unit") or "kg"
+                            
+                            lines_data.append({
+                                "sequence": str(line.get("sequence", "")),
+                                "component_name": component_name,
+                                "component_product_id": line.get("component_product_id", ""),
+                                "quantity": f"{display_qty:.3f}",
+                                "unit": unit,
+                                "notes": line.get("notes", ""),
+                                "density_kg_per_l": density,
+                                "unit_cost": unit_cost,
+                                "base_unit": base_unit
+                            })
+                except Exception as e:
+                    print(f"Error loading assembly lines: {e}")
+                    lines_data = []
+            
+            return (
+                True,  # is_open
+                title,  # title
+                assembly.get("version", 1),  # version
+                assembly_name,  # name
+                assembly.get("is_active", True) == "✓" if isinstance(assembly.get("is_active"), str) else assembly.get("is_active", True),  # active
+                assembly.get("notes", ""),  # notes
+                lines_data,  # lines
+                assembly_id,  # assembly_id
+                product_id if product_id else assembly.get("parent_product_id", "")  # parent_product_id
+            )
+        
+        raise PreventUpdate
+    
+    # Close assembly editor modal
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("assembly-editor-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+        Input("assembly-editor-cancel-btn", "n_clicks"),
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def close_assembly_editor(cancel_clicks):
+        """Close assembly editor modal."""
+        if not cancel_clicks:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        return False
+    
+    # Normalize unit helper function (same as formula)
+    def normalize_unit_assembly(unit_str):
+        """Normalize unit string to domain rules format (uppercase, L not LT)."""
+        if not unit_str:
+            return "KG"
+        unit_upper = str(unit_str).upper()
+        unit_map = {
+            "LT": "L",
+            "LITRE": "L",
+            "LITER": "L",
+            "LITERS": "L",
+            "LITRES": "L",
+        }
+        return unit_map.get(unit_upper, unit_upper)
+    
+    # Calculate live values for assembly editor lines (same as formula)
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-editor-total-lines", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-total-kg", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-total-l", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-total-sg", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-total-cost", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-cost-per-kg", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-editor-cost-per-l", "children")],
+        [Input("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def calculate_assembly_values(lines_data):
+        """Calculate kg, L, cost and totals for each line, and overall totals."""
+        try:
+            from app.domain.rules import to_kg, to_liters, round_money
+            from decimal import Decimal
+            
+            if not lines_data or not isinstance(lines_data, list):
+                return [], "0", "0.000 kg", "0.000 L", "-", "$0.00", "-", "-"
+            
+            import copy
+            updated_lines = copy.deepcopy(lines_data)
+            
+            total_kg = Decimal("0")
+            total_l = Decimal("0")
+            total_cost = Decimal("0")
+            
+            for line in updated_lines:
+                if not isinstance(line, dict):
+                    continue
+                    
+                quantity_str = line.get("quantity", "0")
+                unit = line.get("unit", "kg")
+                density = line.get("density_kg_per_l")
+                unit_cost = line.get("unit_cost")
+                
+                try:
+                    quantity = Decimal(str(quantity_str))
+                except:
+                    quantity = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Convert to kg using domain rules
+                # Only convert if unit is a convertible mass/volume unit
+                kg_value = Decimal("0")
+                normalized_unit = normalize_unit_assembly(unit)
+                
+                # Check if unit is convertible (mass or volume unit)
+                is_mass_unit = normalized_unit in ["MG", "G", "KG", "TON", "OZ", "LB"]
+                is_volume_unit = normalized_unit in ["ML", "L", "LITRE", "LITER"]
+                
+                if quantity > 0 and (is_mass_unit or is_volume_unit):
+                    try:
+                        density_dec = Decimal(str(density)) if density is not None else None
+                        # For volume units, density is required
+                        if is_volume_unit and density_dec is None:
+                            print(f"Warning: Cannot convert {quantity} {unit} to kg - density required")
+                            kg_value = Decimal("0")
+                        else:
+                            result = to_kg(quantity, normalized_unit, density_dec)
+                            kg_value = result.quantity_kg
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"Conversion error for {quantity} {unit}: {e}")
+                        kg_value = Decimal("0")
+                elif quantity > 0:
+                    # Non-convertible unit (ea, pcs, etc.) - cannot convert to kg
+                    print(f"Warning: Unit '{unit}' is not convertible to kg. Quantity will be stored but kg/L calculations skipped.")
+                    kg_value = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Calculate L from kg using density
+                # Only calculate if we have valid kg_value (from convertible units) and density
+                l_value = Decimal("0")
+                if density is not None and kg_value > 0:
+                    try:
+                        density_dec = Decimal(str(density))
+                        if density_dec > 0:
+                            l_value = to_liters(kg_value, density_dec, "L")
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"L conversion error: {e}")
+                        l_value = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Calculate line cost
+                # For cost, we need kg_value for mass-based costing, or use quantity directly for count-based units
+                line_cost = Decimal("0")
+                normalized_unit = normalize_unit_assembly(unit)
+                is_mass_unit = normalized_unit in ["MG", "G", "KG", "TON", "OZ", "LB"]
+                is_volume_unit = normalized_unit in ["ML", "L", "LITRE", "LITER"]
+                
+                if unit_cost is not None:
+                    try:
+                        unit_cost_dec = Decimal(str(unit_cost))
+                        # If we have kg_value (convertible unit), use it for costing
+                        # Otherwise, use quantity directly (for count-based units)
+                        if (is_mass_unit or is_volume_unit) and kg_value > 0:
+                            # Cost per kg × quantity in kg
+                            line_cost = round_money(unit_cost_dec * kg_value)
+                        elif not is_mass_unit and not is_volume_unit:
+                            # For count-based units, assume cost is per unit
+                            # Note: This assumes unit_cost is per each/piece
+                            line_cost = round_money(unit_cost_dec * quantity)
+                    except Exception as e:
+                        print(f"Cost calculation error: {e}")
+                        line_cost = Decimal("0")
+                
+                # Update line with calculated values
+                line["quantity_kg_display"] = float(kg_value)
+                line["quantity_l_display"] = float(l_value) if l_value > 0 else 0.0
+                line["unit_cost_display"] = float(unit_cost) if unit_cost is not None else 0.0
+                line["line_cost_display"] = float(line_cost)
+                
+                # Add to totals
+                total_kg += kg_value
+                if l_value > 0:
+                    total_l += l_value
+                total_cost += line_cost
+            
+            # Calculate assembly SG
+            assembly_sg = Decimal("0")
+            if total_l > 0:
+                assembly_sg = total_kg / total_l
+            
+            total_cost_rounded = round_money(total_cost)
+            
+            # Calculate cost per kg and per L
+            cost_per_kg = Decimal("0")
+            cost_per_l = Decimal("0")
+            
+            if total_kg > 0:
+                cost_per_kg = round_money(total_cost / total_kg)
+            
+            if total_l > 0:
+                cost_per_l = round_money(total_cost / total_l)
+            
+            return (
+                updated_lines,
+                str(len(updated_lines)),
+                f"{float(total_kg):.3f} kg",
+                f"{float(total_l):.3f} L" if float(total_l) > 0 else "-",
+                f"{float(assembly_sg):.6f}" if float(assembly_sg) > 0 else "-",
+                f"${float(total_cost_rounded):.2f}",
+                f"${float(cost_per_kg):.2f}/kg" if float(cost_per_kg) > 0 else "-",
+                f"${float(cost_per_l):.2f}/L" if float(cost_per_l) > 0 else "-"
+            )
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error in calculate_assembly_values: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return [], "0", "0.000 kg", "0.000 L", "-", "$0.00", "-", "-"
+    
+    # Add line to assembly editor
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("assembly-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+        [Input("assembly-add-line-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def add_assembly_line(n_clicks, current_data):
+        """Add a new line to the assembly."""
+        if not n_clicks:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        if current_data is None:
+            current_data = []
+        
+        # Find next sequence number
+        existing_sequences = [int(line.get("sequence", 0)) for line in current_data if line.get("sequence")]
+        next_seq = max(existing_sequences, default=0) + 1 if existing_sequences else 1
+        
+        # Add new line
+        new_line = {
+            "sequence": str(next_seq),
+            "component_name": "[Click to select component]",  # Placeholder
+            "component_product_id": "",  # To be filled when component is selected
+            "quantity": "0.000",
+            "unit": "kg",  # Default unit
+            "notes": ""
+        }
+        
+        return current_data + [new_line]
+    
+    # Edit line - open component selection modal for selected line
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-ingredient-selection-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-current-line-index-store", "children", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("assembly-edit-line-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-editor-lines", "selected_rows"),
+         State("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def edit_assembly_line_component(n_clicks, selected_rows, current_data):
+        """Open component selection modal for selected line."""
+        if not n_clicks or not selected_rows or not current_data:
+            return False, no_update
+        
+        return True, str(selected_rows[0])
+    
+    # Delete line from assembly editor
+    @app.callback(
+        Output("assembly-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+        [Input("assembly-delete-line-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-editor-lines", "selected_rows"),
+         State("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def delete_assembly_line(n_clicks, selected_rows, current_data):
+        """Delete selected line from assembly."""
+        if not n_clicks or not selected_rows or not current_data:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        # Remove selected rows
+        new_data = [row for i, row in enumerate(current_data) if i not in selected_rows]
+        
+        return new_data
+    
+    # Open component selection modal when clicking on component cell
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-ingredient-selection-modal", "is_open"),
+         Output("assembly-current-line-index-store", "children")],
+        [Input("assembly-editor-lines", "active_cell"),
+         Input("assembly-ingredient-modal-cancel", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def open_component_modal(active_cell, cancel_clicks, lines_data):
+        """Open component selection modal when clicking on component column."""
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        trigger_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        
+        # If cancel button clicked, close modal
+        if trigger_id == "assembly-ingredient-modal-cancel":
+            return False, no_update
+        
+        # If clicking on table
+        if active_cell and lines_data:
+            col_id = active_cell.get("column_id")
+            row_idx = active_cell.get("row")
+            
+            # Only open modal if clicking on component column
+            if col_id == "component_name" and row_idx is not None:
+                return True, str(row_idx)
+        
+        return False, no_update
+    
+    # Search components and populate results
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-ingredient-search-results", "children"),
+         Output("assembly-ingredient-search-message", "children")],
+        [Input("assembly-ingredient-search-input", "value")],
+        prevent_initial_call=False
+    )
+    def search_components(search_term):
+        """Search products for components - show ALL active products regardless of type."""
+        # Fetch all active products - don't filter by is_assemble or product_type
+        params = {"is_active": "true"}
+        if search_term and len(search_term) >= 1:
+            params["query"] = search_term
+        
+        # Explicitly ensure we're not filtering by assembly capability
+        # All products should be available as components
+        response = make_api_request("GET", "/products/", data=params)
+        
+        # Handle different response formats
+        if isinstance(response, dict):
+            if "error" in response:
+                return html.Div("Error loading components"), ""
+            elif "products" in response:
+                products = response.get("products", [])
+            else:
+                products = []
+        elif isinstance(response, list):
+            products = response
+        else:
+            products = []
+        
+        message = f"Showing {len(products)} products"
+        
+        if not products:
+            return html.Div(dbc.Alert("No products found", color="warning")), ""
+        
+        # Create table of results
+        results = []
+        for prod in products[:100]:  # Limit to 100 results
+            sku = str(prod.get('sku', '')).strip()
+            name = str(prod.get('name', '')).strip()
+            desc = f"{sku} - {name}".strip()
+            
+            results.append({
+                "id": prod.get("id", ""),
+                "code": sku,
+                "description": desc,
+            })
+        
+        return html.Div([
+            dash_table.DataTable(
+                id="assembly-component-results-table",
+                columns=[
+                    {"name": "SKU", "id": "code"},
+                    {"name": "Name", "id": "description"},
+                ],
+                data=results,
+                row_selectable="single",
+                page_action="native",
+                page_current=0,
+                page_size=20,
+                style_cell={
+                    'textAlign': 'left', 
+                    'fontSize': '11px',
+                    'padding': '8px'
+                },
+                style_header={
+                    'backgroundColor': 'rgb(220, 220, 220)', 
+                    'fontWeight': 'bold'
+                },
+                style_data_conditional=[
+                    {
+                        'if': {'row_index': 'odd'},
+                        'backgroundColor': 'rgb(248, 248, 248)'
+                    }
+                ],
+            )
+        ]), message
+    
+    # Handle component selection from results table
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-editor-lines", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-ingredient-selection-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("assembly-component-results-table", "selected_rows")],
+        [Input("assembly-component-results-table", "selected_rows"),
+         Input("assembly-ingredient-modal-cancel", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-component-results-table", "data"),
+         State("assembly-current-line-index-store", "children"),
+         State("assembly-editor-lines", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def handle_component_selection(selected_rows, cancel_clicks, results_data, line_index, current_lines):
+        """Handle selection of component from results."""
+        ctx = dash.callback_context
+        if not ctx.triggered:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        trigger_id = ctx.triggered[0]["prop_id"].split(".")[0]
+        
+        # If cancel clicked, just close modal
+        if trigger_id == "assembly-ingredient-modal-cancel":
+            return no_update, False, []
+        
+        # If component selected
+        if selected_rows and results_data and current_lines and line_index:
+            selected_row = results_data[selected_rows[0]]
+            component_id = selected_row.get("id")
+            component_name = selected_row.get("description", "")
+            
+            # Fetch full product details including density, cost, and base unit
+            product_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/products/{component_id}")
+            density = None
+            unit_cost = None
+            base_unit = "kg"
+            
+            if not "error" in product_response:
+                density = product_response.get("density_kg_per_l")
+                unit_cost = product_response.get("usage_cost_ex_gst") or product_response.get("usage_cost_inc_gst")
+                base_unit = product_response.get("base_unit") or "kg"
+            
+            # Update the line in assembly editor
+            line_idx = int(line_index)
+            if 0 <= line_idx < len(current_lines):
+                import copy
+                new_lines = copy.deepcopy(current_lines)
+                new_lines[line_idx]["component_product_id"] = component_id
+                new_lines[line_idx]["component_name"] = component_name
+                
+                # Store density, cost, and unit for conversions
+                if density is not None:
+                    new_lines[line_idx]["density_kg_per_l"] = density
+                if unit_cost is not None:
+                    new_lines[line_idx]["unit_cost"] = unit_cost
+                new_lines[line_idx]["base_unit"] = base_unit
+                
+                # Always set unit to component base_unit for consistency
+                new_lines[line_idx]["unit"] = base_unit
+                
+                # Close modal and clear selection
+                return new_lines, False, []
+        
+        return no_update, False, []
+    
+    # Save assembly
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("assembly-editor-modal", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("product-assemblies-table", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "header", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "children", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        [Input("assembly-editor-save-btn", "n_clicks")],
+        [State("assembly-input-name", "value"),
+         State("assembly-input-version", "value"),
+         State("assembly-input-active", "value"),
+         State("assembly-input-notes", "value"),
+         State("assembly-editor-title", "children"),
+         State("assembly-editor-lines", "data"),
+         State("assembly-form-hidden", "children"),
+         State("assembly-parent-product-id-hidden", "children"),
+         State("product-assemblies-table", "selected_rows"),
+         State("product-assemblies-table", "data")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def save_assembly(n_clicks, name, version, is_active, notes, title, lines_data, assembly_id_hidden, parent_product_id, selected_rows, assemblies_data):
+        """Save assembly."""
+        if not n_clicks:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        if not name or not parent_product_id:
+            return False, no_update, True, "Error", "Assembly name and parent product are required"
+        
+        try:
+            from app.domain.rules import to_kg, round_money
+            from decimal import Decimal
+            
+            # Determine if this is edit mode or duplicate mode
+            is_edit = title == "Edit Assembly" and assembly_id_hidden and str(assembly_id_hidden).strip()
+            is_duplicate = title == "Duplicate Assembly"
+            assembly_id = str(assembly_id_hidden).strip() if assembly_id_hidden else None
+            
+            # Convert lines data to API format
+            lines = []
+            if lines_data:
+                for line in lines_data:
+                    component_product_id = line.get("component_product_id", "")
+                    if not component_product_id:
+                        continue
+                    
+                    quantity = float(line.get("quantity", 0))
+                    unit = line.get("unit", "kg")
+                    
+                    # Convert to kg using density if available
+                    # Only convert if unit is convertible (mass or volume unit)
+                    normalized_unit = normalize_unit_assembly(unit)
+                    is_mass_unit = normalized_unit in ["MG", "G", "KG", "TON", "OZ", "LB"]
+                    is_volume_unit = normalized_unit in ["ML", "L", "LITRE", "LITER"]
+                    
+                    quantity_kg = quantity  # Default fallback
+                    if is_mass_unit or is_volume_unit:
+                        try:
+                            density = line.get("density_kg_per_l")
+                            density_dec = Decimal(str(density)) if density is not None else None
+                            # For volume units, density is required
+                            if is_volume_unit and density_dec is None:
+                                print(f"Warning: Cannot convert {quantity} {unit} to kg - density required. Using fallback.")
+                                quantity_kg = quantity  # Can't convert without density
+                            else:
+                                result = to_kg(Decimal(str(quantity)), normalized_unit, density_dec)
+                                quantity_kg = float(result.quantity_kg)
+                        except Exception as e:
+                            print(f"Error converting quantity {quantity} {unit}: {e}")
+                            quantity_kg = quantity
+                    else:
+                        # Non-convertible unit (ea, pcs, etc.) - cannot convert to kg
+                        # For now, we'll store the quantity as-is, but this may need review
+                        print(f"Warning: Unit '{unit}' is not convertible to kg. Storing quantity as-is.")
+                        quantity_kg = quantity
+                    
+                    # Ensure sequence is at least 1 for API validation
+                    seq = int(line.get("sequence", 0))
+                    if seq < 1:
+                        seq = 1
+                    
+                    lines.append({
+                        "component_product_id": component_product_id,
+                        "quantity": quantity_kg,
+                        "sequence": seq,
+                        "notes": line.get("notes", ""),
+                        "unit": line.get("unit", "kg"),
+                        "is_energy_or_overhead": False  # Required field
+                    })
+            
+            if is_edit:
+                # Update existing assembly
+                payload = {
+                    "assembly_name": name,
+                    "is_active": is_active,
+                    "notes": notes,
+                    "version": version or 1,
+                    "lines": lines
+                }
+                response = make_api_request("PUT", f"/assemblies/{assembly_id}", payload)
+            else:
+                # Create new assembly - generate assembly_code
+                all_assemblies = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={parent_product_id}")
+                existing_codes = []
+                if isinstance(all_assemblies, list):
+                    for a in all_assemblies:
+                        code = a.get("assembly_code", "")
+                        if code:
+                            existing_codes.append(code)
+                
+                # Generate code from parent product SKU + sequence
+                parent_product = make_api_request("GET", f"/products/{parent_product_id}")
+                parent_sku = parent_product.get("sku", "ASSY") if isinstance(parent_product, dict) else "ASSY"
+                base_code = f"{parent_sku}-ASSY"
+                assembly_code = base_code
+                counter = 1
+                while assembly_code in existing_codes:
+                    assembly_code = f"{base_code}-{counter}"
+                    counter += 1
+                
+                payload = {
+                    "parent_product_id": parent_product_id,
+                    "assembly_code": assembly_code,
+                    "assembly_name": name,
+                    "version": version or 1,
+                    "is_primary": False,  # Set primary separately
+                    "is_active": is_active,
+                    "notes": notes,
+                    "lines": lines
+                }
+                response = make_api_request("POST", "/assemblies/", payload)
+            
+            # Check for errors - response might be dict with error key or direct error
+            error_occurred = False
+            error_msg = "Unknown error"
+            
+            if isinstance(response, dict):
+                if "error" in response:
+                    error_occurred = True
+                    error_msg = response.get("error", "Unknown error")
+                    if isinstance(error_msg, str):
+                        try:
+                            import json
+                            error_obj = json.loads(error_msg)
+                            if "message" in error_obj:
+                                error_msg = error_obj["message"]
+                        except:
+                            pass
+                elif "detail" in response:
+                    # FastAPI error format
+                    error_occurred = True
+                    error_msg = response.get("detail", "Unknown error")
+                    if isinstance(error_msg, str):
+                        try:
+                            import json
+                            error_obj = json.loads(error_msg)
+                            if "message" in error_obj:
+                                error_msg = error_obj["message"]
+                        except:
+                            pass
+            
+            if error_occurred:
+                # Extract details if available (for validation errors)
+                details = response.get("details", [])
+                if details:
+                    detail_msgs = []
+                    for detail in details:
+                        field = detail.get("field", "unknown")
+                        msg = detail.get("message", "invalid")
+                        detail_msgs.append(f"{field}: {msg}")
+                    error_msg_with_details = f"{error_msg}. Details: {'; '.join(detail_msgs)}"
+                    print(f"Error saving assembly: {error_msg_with_details}")
+                    print(f"Full error response: {response}")
+                    return False, no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to save assembly: {error_msg_with_details}"
+                else:
+                    print(f"Error saving assembly: {error_msg}")
+                    print(f"Full error response: {response}")
+                    return False, no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to save assembly: {error_msg}"
+            
+            # Success - response should contain the saved assembly or success indicator
+            print(f"Assembly save successful. Response: {response}")
+            
+            # Reload assemblies to refresh the table
+            assemblies_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={parent_product_id}")
+            print(f"Reloaded assemblies response: {assemblies_response}")
+            
+            # Handle different response formats
+            if isinstance(assemblies_response, dict) and "error" in assemblies_response:
+                # Error loading assemblies, but save was successful
+                print(f"Warning: Could not reload assemblies: {assemblies_response.get('error')}")
+                assemblies = []
+            elif isinstance(assemblies_response, list):
+                assemblies = assemblies_response
+            elif isinstance(assemblies_response, dict) and "assemblies" in assemblies_response:
+                assemblies = assemblies_response.get("assemblies", [])
+            else:
+                assemblies = []
+            
+            # Format for table display - remove nested fields
+            table_data = format_assemblies_for_table(assemblies)
+            
+            success_msg = "Assembly updated successfully" if is_edit else "Assembly created successfully"
+            print(f"Returning success with {len(table_data)} assemblies")
+            return False, table_data, True, "Success", success_msg
+            
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Error saving assembly: {e}")
+            import traceback
+            traceback.print_exc()
+            return False, no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to save assembly: {str(e)}"
+    
+    # Set primary assembly
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("product-assemblies-table", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "header", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "children", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        Input("set-primary-assembly-btn", "n_clicks"),
+        [State("product-assemblies-table", "selected_rows"),
+         State("product-assemblies-table", "data"),
+         State("product-form-hidden", "children")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def set_primary_assembly(n_clicks, selected_rows, assemblies_data, product_id_hidden):
+        """Set selected assembly as primary (deactivates others)."""
+        if not n_clicks or not selected_rows or not assemblies_data:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        assembly = assemblies_data[selected_rows[0]]
+        assembly_id = assembly.get("id")
+        parent_product_id = product_id_hidden.strip() if product_id_hidden else assembly.get("parent_product_id", "")
+        
+        if not assembly_id:
+            return no_update, True, "Error", "Assembly ID not found"
+        
+        try:
+            # Set as primary via API
+            response = make_api_request("POST", f"/assemblies/{assembly_id}/set-primary")
+            if isinstance(response, dict) and "error" in response:
+                return no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to set primary: {response.get('error', 'Unknown error')}"
+            
+            # Reload assemblies
+            assemblies_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={parent_product_id}")
+            assemblies = assemblies_response if isinstance(assemblies_response, list) else []
+            
+            # Format for table display - remove nested fields
+            table_data = format_assemblies_for_table(assemblies)
+            
+            return table_data, True, "Success", "Primary assembly set successfully"
+        
+        except Exception as e:
+            return no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to set primary: {str(e)}"
+    
+    # Archive assembly
+    @app.callback(
+        [Output("product-assemblies-table", "data", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "is_open", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "header", allow_duplicate=True),
+         Output("toast", "children", allow_duplicate=True)],
+        Input("archive-assembly-btn", "n_clicks"),
+        [State("product-assemblies-table", "selected_rows"),
+         State("product-assemblies-table", "data"),
+         State("product-form-hidden", "children")],
+        prevent_initial_call=True
+    )
+    def archive_assembly(n_clicks, selected_rows, assemblies_data, product_id_hidden):
+        """Archive selected assembly by setting is_active to False."""
+        if not n_clicks or not selected_rows or not assemblies_data:
+            raise PreventUpdate
+        
+        assembly = assemblies_data[selected_rows[0]]
+        assembly_id = assembly.get("id")
+        parent_product_id = product_id_hidden.strip() if product_id_hidden else assembly.get("parent_product_id", "")
+        
+        if not assembly_id:
+            return no_update, True, "Error", "Assembly ID not found"
+        
+        try:
+            # Update assembly to set is_active = False
+            payload = {"is_active": False}
+            response = make_api_request("PUT", f"/assemblies/{assembly_id}", payload)
+            if isinstance(response, dict) and "error" in response:
+                return no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to archive assembly: {response.get('error', 'Unknown error')}"
+            
+            # Reload assemblies
+            assemblies_response = make_api_request("GET", f"/assemblies/?parent_product_id={parent_product_id}")
+            assemblies = assemblies_response if isinstance(assemblies_response, list) else []
+            
+            # Format for table display - remove nested fields
+            table_data = format_assemblies_for_table(assemblies)
+            
+            return table_data, True, "Success", "Assembly archived successfully"
+        
+        except Exception as e:
+            return no_update, True, "Error", f"Failed to archive assembly: {str(e)}"

+### Assembly Model
+**Purpose**: Product-specific component lists for costing and BOM generation
+
+An **Assembly** links a parent product (output) to child products (components), supporting:
+- **Multiple versions per product**: e.g., internal vs external canning operations
+- **Primary designation**: `is_primary=True` marks the default assembly for costing
+- **Cost basis differentiation**: `is_energy_or_overhead` flag for energy/overhead costs
+- **Yield adjustments**: `yield_factor` for expected efficiency (default 1.0 = 100%)
+- **Temporal validity**: `effective_from/to` for date-based assembly switching
+- **Sequence ordering**: `sequence` for multi-step assembly operations
+
+**Key Fields:**
+- `parent_product_id`: Output product (e.g., "RTD Can")
+- `child_product_id`: Component product (e.g., "Can", "Lid", "Contents")
+- `ratio`: Quantity of child per parent
+- `is_primary`: Boolean - primary assembly for theoretical costing
+- `version`: Integer - assembly version tracking
+- `notes`: Assembly-specific notes
+
+**Example Use Case (RTD Can)**:
+- RTD Can (parent) → Can product, Lid product, Canning Cost, Contents
+- Version 1: Internal canning operation (cost: internal labor + materials)
+- Version 2: External canning operation (cost: contract price + contents)
+
+### Quality Test Definition Model
+**Purpose**: Pre-defined quality tests for batch QC
+
+**QualityTestDefinition** provides reusable test templates:
+- `code`, `name`: Test identification
+- `test_type`: numeric, pass_fail, text, etc.
+- `unit`: Unit of measurement
+- `min_value`, `max_value`: Acceptable range
+- `target_value`: Target for numeric tests
+- `is_active`: Active/archived status
+
+**QC Results** link to test definitions via `test_definition_id`, with denormalized `test_name` and `test_unit` for display.
+
+### Work Order Model Extensions
+**New Fields:**
+- `instructions`: Manufacturing instructions (copied from formula or overridden)
+
+### Work Order Line Model Extensions
+**New Fields:**
+- `actual_quantity_kg`: Actually consumed in production (captured during execution)
+
+### Formula Model Extensions
+**New Fields:**
+- `instructions`: Production instructions for this recipe version
+
 ### DDL
-> See `db/alembic/` migrations driven from SQLAlchemy models. The schema includes: **unified products** (with product_type: RAW/WIP/FINISHED), variants, formulas/lines (using unified product_id), inventory lots/txns (FIFO), assemblies, WOs, batches, QC, suppliers/POs, customers/SOs, **invoices**, **pricing** (lists + overrides), **pack units** & **conversions**.
+> See `db/alembic/` migrations driven from SQLAlchemy models. The schema includes: **unified products** (with product_type: RAW/WIP/FINISHED), **assemblies** (product-specific BOMs with versions and primary designation), **quality test definitions**, variants, formulas/lines (using unified product_id, with instructions), inventory lots/txns (FIFO with cost sources), work orders/lines (with instructions and actual vs required quantities), batches (with actual vs theoretical yields), QC (linked to test definitions), suppliers/POs, customers/SOs, **invoices**, **pricing** (lists + overrides), **pack units** & **conversions**.
